"BONUS MOD CONTAINS EXTRA ENEMIES MOD WHICH CONTAINS ADVENTURERS MOD - No need to mix these mods." inherit IMP {}

"ADVENTURER"
  {
    viewId = { "player" }
    attr = {
      DAMAGE 15
      DEFENSE 20 
    }
    body = {
      type = Humanoid LARGE
    }
    name = {
      name = "squire"
      firstNameGen = "FIRST_MALE"
      fullTitle = true
     }
    permanentEffects = {
      AMBUSH_SKILL 1
      RIDER 1
    }
    maxLevelIncrease = {
      DAMAGE 16
      SPELL_DAMAGE 16
      RANGED_DAMAGE 16
    }
    hatedByEffect = HATE_HUMANS
    spellSchools = { "fighter" "mage" }
    inventory = {
      { "FirstAidKit" 2 4 }
      { "Knife"}
      { "Sword"}
      { "LeatherGloves"}
      { "LeatherArmor"}
      { "LeatherHelm"}
      { "GoldPiece" 16 26 }
    }
  }
"ADVENTURER_F" inherit "ADVENTURER"
  {
    viewId = { "player_f" }
    gender = FEMALE
    name = {
      name = "squire"
      firstNameGen = "FIRST_FEMALE"
      fullTitle = true
     }
  }

"CAT1"
  {
    viewId = { "cat01" }
    attr = {
      DAMAGE 5
      DEFENSE 5 
    }
    body = {
      type = FourLegged MEDIUM
      intrinsicAttacks = {
        HEAD {{{ Intrinsic { "bite_attack" }  "fangs" 4 { attackType = BITE attackMsg = BITE } }}}
      }
      weight = 10
    }
    aiType = RANGED
    name = {
      name = "cat"
    }
    chatReactionFriendly = "mews knowingly"
    chatReactionHostile = "\"HISSS!\""
    petReaction = "purrs"
  }

   "BONUS_BUFF_TOTEM"
   {
    viewId = { "bufftotem_creature" }
    attr = {
     DAMAGE 0
     DEFENSE 20
     }
     body = {
       type = NonHumanoid LARGE
       material = WOOD
       weight = 550
       addBodyPart = {
           BACK 2
           HEAD 1
             } }
      spells = {
        "BONUS_haste other"
        "BONUS_defend other"
        "BONUS_friendly damage bonus"
      }
      permanentEffects = {
        IMMOBILE 1
        SLOWED 1
        RANGED_RESISTANCE 1
        POISON_RESISTANT 1
        SLEEP_RESISTANT 1
      }
      cantEquip = true
      name = {
        name = "buff totem"
      }
      chatReactionFriendly = "\"A wooden buff totem. \""
      chatReactionHostile = "\"A wooden buff totem.\""
      deathDescription = "destroyed"
    }

	#Recruitable Dwarf Miners!
	#Intended for Lawful/Castle Keepers to hire so you don't have to conquer & enslave!
	#Stole a lot from the DWARF_WORKER.
	"BONUS_DWARF_MINER" inherit "DWARF"
	{
		viewId = {"dwarf_miner"}
		attr = {
		DAMAGE 12 #These folks are intended to stand up to lava golems, base DEF 36.
		DEFENSE 35 #LG base dmg/fire-dmg 26/36. There is probably some adjustment for z-depth.
		DIGGING 55
		FURNACE 40
		}
		body = {
			type = Humanoid MEDIUM
			weight = 100
			intrinsicAttacks = {
				ARM {{
				isExtraAttack = true
				itemType = { Intrinsic { "fist_attack" } "pickaxe" 5 {
				attackType = HIT
				attackMsg = SWING } }}}
			}
		}
		inventory = {
			{ "LeatherArmor"}
			{ type = "LeatherHelm" chance = 0.5 }
			{ type = "LeatherBoots" chance = 0.5 }
			{ type = "Torch" chance = 1.0 }
		}
		name = {
        name = "dwarf miner"
        pluralName = "dwarven miners"
        firstNameGen = "DWARF"
		}
      maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 12 } #Lots of training capacity still doesn't make them good fighters, but it does let them survive more effectively in hellish mining conditions.
      permanentEffects = {
        MAGIC_VULNERABILITY 1
        NO_CARRY_LIMIT 1
		REGENERATION 1 #As does regen.
      }
	  chatReactionFriendly = "curses murderous animating molten-rock walls"
      chatReactionHostile = "\"Die!\""
	}

"BONUS_DWARF_MILITIA_TRIBE" inherit "BONUS_DWARF_MILITIA"
{
      inventory = {
        { type =  "BONUS_SteelSword" prefixChance = 0.05 }
        { countMin = 1 countMax = 2 type = Potion Heal {FLESH} chance = 0.2 }
        { type =  "LeatherArmor" prefixChance = 0.05 }
        {  "LeatherBoots" }
        {  "WoodenShield" }
        { type =  "Torch" chance = 0.1 }
        { countMin = 4 countMax = 8 type =  "GoldPiece" chance = 0.6 }
        { type =  "BONUS_DwarvenBeer" chance = 0.1 }
      }
}

      }
    }
  "BONUS_DWARF_QUEEN_TRIBE" inherit "BONUS_DWARF_QUEEN"
    {
      attr = {
        DAMAGE 40
        DEFENSE 38 
      }
	  maxLevelIncrease = {
        DAMAGE 4
	  }
	  spells = { "advanced healing" "BONUS_area defense bonus" "BONUS_area damage bonus" }
	  inventory = {
       { type =  "BONUS_InfWarHammer", alternative =  "AdaWarHammer" prefixChance = 1 }
	   { type =  "BONUS_InfArmor", alternative =  "AdaArmor" prefixChance = 0.9 }
       { type =  "BONUS_InfBoots", alternative =  "AdaBoots" prefixChance = 0.8 }
       { type =  "BONUS_InfGloves", alternative =  "AdaGloves" prefixChance = 0.7 }
	   { type =  "BONUS_InfHelm", alternative =  "AdaHelm" prefixChance = 0.65 chance = 0.8 }
       { type = Scroll IncreaseAttr DAMAGE 2 countMin = 1 countMax = 1 chance = 0.5 }
	   { type = Potion IncreaseAttr RANGED_DAMAGE 1 countMin = 1 countMax = 1  chance = 0.5 }
       { type = Scroll IncreaseAttr DEFENSE 2 countMin = 1 countMax = 1  chance = 0.5 }
	   { type = Potion IncreaseAttr SPELL_DAMAGE 1 countMin = 1 countMax = 1  chance = 0.5 }
	   { type = Glyph {ARMOR LastingEffect MELEE_RESISTANCE}  chance = 0.1 }
	   { type = Glyph {ARMOR LastingEffect REGENERATION} chance = 0.05 }
	   { type = Glyph {WEAPON ItemAttrBonus DAMAGE 4} chance = 0.3 }
       {  "GoldPiece" 65 88 }
	   { Potion Permanent SPEED 1 1 1 }
	   { Potion RegrowBodyPart 1 1 1 1 }
	   { Scroll Permanent LIGHT_SOURCE 1 1 0.4 }
       { Potion Heal {FLESH} 2 3 }
      }
 	}

###
#Allow several creatures to take basic melee training, mostly so they can defend a little better. A37 defaults to combat XP helping melee performance unless other categories are identified, so it's not critical for that purpose anymore.  Yay!
"WITCHMAN" modify append { maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 7 } }
#Witchers seemed pretty useless last I converted one. Hoping this helps.
"KOBOLD" modify append { maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 3 } }
"GOBLIN_ARTIFICER" modify append { maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 3 } }
"ARTISAN" modify append { maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 3 } }
#Your gear-builders needn't be great fighters, but if you're building weapons & armor it helps to know how to use said weapons & armor.
"SOFT_MONSTER" modify append { maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 3 } }
#If you meet the Soft Monster in a dungeon, it'd be nice if he trained up after conversion.
"GOBLIN_MATRON" modify append { maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 5 } }
"BONUS_GOBLIN_MATRON_PLAYER" modify append {maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 5  } }
#Children may be grounds for complaint...but I'm pretty sure the matrons would defend them, since they gear up for combat

#Combat steeds should be able to benefit from *some* training.
#"WARHORSE" modify append {maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 3 } }
"BONUS_LION" modify append {maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 1 } }
"BONUS_LIONESS" modify append {	maxLevelIncrease = { DAMAGE 1 } }

#Dragons have their own names and language, so they're clearly intelligent, so they should be able to train. Balancing is tricky, though.
"GREEN_DRAGON" modify append {	 maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 7} }
"RED_DRAGON" modify append {	 maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 7} }
"BLACK_DRAGON" modify append {	 maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 7} }
"WHITE_DRAGON" modify append {	 maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 7} }
"YELLOW_DRAGON" modify append {	 maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 7} }

#Since zombies & skeletons can train in vanilla, I guess the dragons can as well.
"BONUS_ZOMBIE_DRAGON" modify append {	 maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 7} }
"BONE_DRAGON" modify append {	 maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 7} }

#Ancient dragons have seen it all already, or at least they'd think so.
"BONUS_ANCIENT_GREEN_DRAGON" modify append {maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 3} }
"BONUS_ANCIENT_RED_DRAGON" modify append {maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 3} }

#Young dragons, however, can learn a lot!
"BONUS_YOUNG_GREEN_DRAGON" modify append {maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 14} }
"BONUS_YOUNG_RED_DRAGON" modify append {maxLevelIncrease = {DAMAGE 14} }
####

#Making absolutely sure farming creatures can farm; didn't cause immediately-noticeable errors on my end
"IMP" modify { permanentEffects = append { CROPS_SKILL 1 } }
"PESEANT_PLAYER" modify { permanentEffects = append { CROPS_SKILL 1 } }
"GOBLIN_WORKER" modify { permanentEffects = append { CROPS_SKILL 1 } }

"GOODWIZ_KEEPER_MAGE_ARCANE"
  {
    # Definitions in tiles.txt
    viewId = { "arcane_keeper_1" }
    # ViewId upgrades of Keepers are applied every 5 tech level increases
    viewIdUpgrades = { { "arcane_keeper_2" } { "arcane_keeper_3" } { "arcane_keeper_4" } }
    name = {
      # The name gets changed appropriately to Keeper and Adventurer
      name = "wizard"
      # Definitions in name_generator.h
      firstNameGen = "FIRST_MALE"
      # Creature is always referred to as [FirstName] the [Creature name]
      fullTitle = true
    }
    body = {
      # One of Humanoid, HumanoidLike, Bird, FourLegged and NonHumanoid
      # size is one of SMALL, MEDIUM, LARGE and HUGE, influences stuff like pushing boulders and being pushed
      type = Humanoid LARGE
    }
    # attr_type.h
    attr = {
      DAMAGE 12
      DEFENSE 12
      SPELL_DAMAGE 20
	  LABORATORY 10
    }   
	permanentEffects = {
      RIDER 1
    }
    # experience_type.h
    maxLevelIncrease = {
      DAMAGE 7
      SPELL_DAMAGE 12
    }
    aiType = RANGED
    spellSchools = { "mage" }
    spells = { "healing" }
    inventory = {
      # Here comes a list of items. The format of each element is defined in creature_inventory.h
      { "Robe"}
	  { "WoodenStaff" }
      # Take a look a CYCLOPS for a more detailed example.
    }
  }

		 }
		}
	   }

"SST_FK_WAR_WOLF"
{
	viewId = { "wolf" }
	attr = {
	DAMAGE 25
	DEFENSE 20
	}
	#There's only so much you can do to armor a wolf that's also gonna carry an armored rider.  This is mostly training & breeding.
	#Conversely, gave 'em a boost to help keep up with A37.
	body = {
      type = FourLegged MEDIUM
      weight = 35
      intrinsicAttacks = {
        LEG  {{itemType = { Intrinsic { "claws_attack" } "claws" 8 { attackType = HIT attackMsg = CLAW } } isExtraAttack = true }}
        HEAD {{itemType = { Intrinsic { "bite_attack" }  "fangs" 7 { attackType = BITE attackMsg = BITE} } isExtraAttack = true }}
      }
    }
	#The stat-ups for war wolves already take some training into account. Steed training on dummies will likely represent time spent acclimating to your creatures,
	#getting the tack well-fitted, and probably teaching the best available fighting skills as well.
	maxLevelIncrease = {
		DAMAGE 4
	}
	#In particular, war wolves don't go exploring around. This is why they aren't an inherit from WOLF.
	permanentEffects = {
      	NIGHT_VISION 1
      	STEED 1
		SWARMER 1
    	} #War wolves might not be individually as impressive as a warg...but they *are* pack hunters.
	
	#War wolves are happy in their role
	chatReactionFriendly = "barks happily."
    chatReactionHostile = "growls angrily."
	petReaction = "wags its tail happily."
	
      name = {
      name = "war wolf"
      pluralName = "wolves"
      groupName = "pack"
    }
}

		MAGIC_RESISTANCE 1
    	}
	noChase = true #Rescue dogs stay with their rescuee.
    aiType = MELEE
    name = {
      name = "rescue dog"
      groupName = "pack"
      firstNameGen = "DOG"
    }
    chatReactionFriendly = "listens attentively."
    chatReactionHostile = "barks and blocks the way."
	petReaction = "appreciates your help with the heavy harness, wagging happily."
  }
 
  ###
  #NB Keeper Creatures
  ###
  "KEEPER_MAGE_NB"
  {
    # Definitions in tiles.txt
    viewId = { "keeper1NB" }
    # ViewId upgrades of Keepers are applied every 5 tech level increases
	##
	# Add the Rgb string after each viewId if you want to pick a color, forex BonusMod Hard Mode Purple: viewId = { "keeper1NB" Rgb 106 106 255 106 }
	# For the record: Rgb values are Red Grn Blu Alpha, in that order.  Not always obvious!
	# Rgb 67 212 220 255 is the Bright Blue from VanillaRetiles. Little too bright for full-body though.
	# Rgb 42 124 162 255 is the Dark Blue, works OK as a full-body for Good-Aligned.
	# Rgb 231 231 231 255 is Vanilla Retiles Generic Shiny Armor Grey.
	# Rgb 54 54 54 255 is Necromancer Faded Black.
	##
    viewIdUpgrades = { { "keeper2NB" } { "keeper3NB" } { "keeper4NB" } }
    name = {
      name = "wizard"
      firstNameGen = "DEITY"
      fullTitle = true
    }
	gender = IT
    body = {
      # One of Humanoid, HumanoidLike, Bird, FourLegged and NonHumanoid
      # size is one of SMALL, MEDIUM, LARGE and HUGE, influences stuff like pushing boulders and being pushed
      type = Humanoid LARGE
    }
    # attr_type.h
    attr = {
      DAMAGE 12
      DEFENSE 12
      SPELL_DAMAGE 20
      LABORATORY 10
    }
    # lasting_effect.h
    permanentEffects = {
      RIDER 1
    }
    # attr_type.h
    maxLevelIncrease = {
      DAMAGE 7
      SPELL_DAMAGE 12
    }
    aiType = RANGED
    spellSchools = { "mage" }
    spells = { "healing" }
    inventory = {
      # Here comes a list of items. The format of each element is defined in creature_inventory.h
      { "Robe"}
      { "WoodenStaff" }
      # Take a look a CYCLOPS for a more detailed example.
    }
  }
